Motion}}","\\end{center}","\\begin{itemize}","\\item For example, if you use \\ttfamily{d2w} \\normalfont{,} it will delete 2 words.\\\\","\\item If you do not use any range, it will automatically set it to 1. Also some verb can be used repeatedly.\\\\","\\item Also certain words allow \\ttfamily{i} \\normalfont{to} be a range which i stands for \"inner.\" This allows you to have your","cursor located anywhere on a word and be able to edit the whole word instead of just your cursor to the","end of the word. For example, if your cursor was in the middle of a word and you enter \\ttfamily{dw}\\normalfont{,} you will","delete only from your cursor to the end of the word. <div id="LC9" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-k">\usepackage</span>{<span class="pl-c1">anysize</span>}</div>
<div id="LC10" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\marginsize</span>{14pt}{12pt}{0pt}{20pt}</div>
<div id="LC11" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\pagestyle</span>{fancy}</div>
<div id="LC12" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-k">\renewcommand</span><span class="pl-c1">\headrule</span>{}</div>
<div id="LC13" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\rhead</span>{UCR-CS100FALL}</div>
<div id="LC14" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">
</div>
<div id="LC15" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{<span class="pl-smi">document</span>}</div>
<div id="LC16" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{<span class="pl-smi">center</span>}</div>
<div id="LC17" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\LARGE</span><span class="pl-c1">\textbf</span>{<span class="pl-mb">Vim Cheatsheet</span>}<span class="pl-c1">\\</span></div>
<div id="LC18" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\textit</span>{<span class="pl-mi">Itsuki David Fukada, Jesus Christian Reyes</span>}</div>
<div id="LC19" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\end</span>{<span class="pl-smi">center</span>}</div>
<div id="LC20" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">
</div>
<div id="LC21" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{<span class="pl-smi">framed</span>}</div>
<div id="LC22" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{<span class="pl-smi">center</span>}</div>
<div id="LC23" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\Large</span><span class="pl-c1">\textbf</span>{<span class="pl-mb">Format of command is: <span class="pl-c1">\ttfamily</span>{Verb Range Motion}</span>}</div>
<div id="LC24" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\end</span>{<span class="pl-smi">center</span>}</div>
<div id="LC25" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{<span class="pl-smi">itemize</span>}</div>
<div id="LC26" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-k">\item</span> For example, if you use <span class="pl-c1">\ttfamily</span>{d2w} <span class="pl-c1">\normalfont</span>{,} it will delete 2 words.<span class="pl-c1">\\</span></div>
<div id="LC27" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-k">\item</span> If you do not use any range, it will automatically set it to 1. Also some verb can be used repeatedly.<span class="pl-c1">\\</span></div>
<div id="LC28" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-k">\item</span> Also certain words allow <span class="pl-c1">\ttfamily</span>{i} <span class="pl-c1">\normalfont</span>{to} be a range which i stands for <span class="pl-ii">&quot;inner.&quot;</span> This allows you to have your</div>
<div id="LC29" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">cursor located anywhere on a word and be able to edit the whole word instead of just your cursor to the</div>
<div id="LC30" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">end of the word. For example, if your cursor was in the middle of a word and you enter <span class="pl-c1">\ttfamily</span>{dw}<span class="pl-c1">\normalfont</span>{,} you will</div>
<div id="LC31" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">delete only from your cursor to the end of the word. If you entered <span class="pl-c1">\ttfamily</span>{diw}<span class="pl-c1">\normalfont</span>{,} you will delete the whole word.</div>
<div id="LC32" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-k">\item</span> To exit insert or visual mode use <span class="pl-c1">\textless</span> Esc<span class="pl-c1">\textgreater</span> <span class="pl-c1">\\</span></div>
<div id="LC33" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\end</span>{<span class="pl-smi">itemize</span>}</div>
<div id="LC34" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\end</span>{<span class="pl-smi">framed</span>}</div>
<div id="LC35" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{<span class="pl-smi">multicols</span>}{2}</div>
<div id="LC36" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{<span class="pl-smi">center</span>}</div>
<div id="LC37" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\textbf</span>{<span class="pl-mb"><span class="pl-c1">\LARGE</span>{Verb/Editing}</span>}<span class="pl-c1">\\</span></div>
<div id="LC38" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\end</span>{<span class="pl-smi">center</span>}</div>
<div id="LC39" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\large</span><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{<span class="pl-smi">tabular</span>}{lll}</div>
<div id="LC40" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\ttfamily</span>{i} &amp; Insert mode at current cursor\\</div>
<div id="LC41" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\ttfamily</span>{I} &amp; Insert mode at beginning of line\\</div>
<div id="LC42" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\ttfamily</span>{a} &amp; Insert mode after the cursor\\</div>
<div id="LC43" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\ttfamily</span>{A} &amp; Insert mode at end of line\\</div>
<div id="LC44" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\ttfamily</span>{o} &amp; Append a new line below the current\\</div>
<div id="LC45" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">&amp; line\\</div>
<div id="LC46" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\ttfamily</span>{O} &amp; Append a new line above the current\\</div>
<div id="LC47" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">&amp; line\\</div>
<div id="LC48" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\ttfamily</span>{s} &amp; Delete word and enter insert mode\\</div>
<div id="LC49" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\ttfamily</span>{S} &amp; Delete line and enter insert mode\\</div>
<div id="LC50" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\ttfamily</span>{f+CHARACTER} &amp; Finds first instance of <span class="pl-c1">\ttfamily</span>{CHARACTER}\\</div>
<div id="LC51" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\ttfamily</span>{r} &amp; Replace a single character\\</div>
<div id="LC52" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\ttfamily</span>{J} &amp; Join the line below with the current\\</div>
<div id="LC53" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\ttfamily</span>{c} &amp; Replace (combine with Motion and/or\\<span class="pl-cce">\</span></div>
<div id="LC54" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">&amp; Range)\\</div>
<div id="LC55" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\ttfamily</span>{x} &amp; Deletes the character at current cursor\\</div>
<div id="LC56" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">&amp; (cut)\\</div>
<div id="LC57" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\ttfamily</span>{d} &amp; Delete (cut)\\</div>
<div id="LC58" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\ttfamily</span>{D} &amp; Deletes from cursor to end of line\\</div>
<div id="LC59" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\ttfamily</span>{y} &amp; Yank the highlighted text (copy)\\</div>
<div id="LC60" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\ttfamily</span>{p} &amp; Paste the clipboard\\</div>
<div id="LC61" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\ttfamily</span>{u} &amp; Undo\\</div>
<div id="LC62" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\ttfamily</span>{U} &amp; Undos entire line\\</div>
<div id="LC63" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div ">&amp; original state\\</div>
<div id="LC64" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\ttfamily</span>{Ctrl+r} &amp; Redo\\</div>
<div id="LC65" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\ttfamily</span>{<span class="pl-c1">\textgreater</span>} &amp; Indent to the right\\</div>
<div id="LC66" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\ttfamily</span>{<span class="pl-c1">\textless</span>} &amp; Indent to the left\\</div>
<div id="LC67" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\ttfamily</span><span class="pl-c1">\url</span>{~} &amp; Changes character&#39;s case\\</div>
<div id="LC68" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\ttfamily</span>{Ctrl-u} &amp; Scroll Up\\</div>
<div id="LC69" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\ttfamily</span>{Ctrl-d} &amp; Scroll down\\</div>
<div id="LC70" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\ttfamily</span>{Ctrl-y} <span class="pl-c1">\normalfont</span>{(Yore)} &amp; Scroll up one line\\</div>
<div id="LC71" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\ttfamily</span>{Ctrl-e} <span class="pl-c1">\normalfont</span>{(Efter)} &amp; Scroll down one line\\</div>
<div id="LC72" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\end</span>{<span class="pl-smi">tabular</span>}</div>

<div id="LC101" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-c1">\ttfamily</span>{H} &amp; (High)Go to top of visible page\\</div>

<div id="LC151" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{<span class="pl-smi">center</span>}</span></div>

<div id="LC157" class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents-no-virtualization react-file-line html-div "><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-c1">\ttfamily</span>{:tabe} &amp; Creates a new tab\\</span></div>
